## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

```
A wide quote card featuring a famous person, with a brown background and a light-gold serif font for the quote: â€œ{argument name="famous_quote" default="Stay Hungry, Stay Foolish"}â€ and smaller text: â€œâ€”{argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}.â€ There is a large, subtle quotation mark before the text. The portrait of the person is on the left, the text on the right. The text occupies two-thirds of the image and the portrait one-third, with a slight gradient transition effect on the portrait.
```

### No. 2: Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

Create an Infographics with bento grid 8 module layout, user can specify any product name in Food, Medicine, tech etc category, choose language, Background style, Hero grid style

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Input Variable: [insert product name]
Language: [insert language]

System Instruction:
Create an image of premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules (card 2 to 8 show text titles only).
1) Product Analysis:
â†’ Identify product's dominant natural color â†’ "hero color"
â†’ Identify category: FOOD / MEDICINE / TECH
2) Color Palette (derived from hero):
â†’ Product + accents: full saturation hero color
â†’ Icons, borders: muted hero (30-40% saturation, never black)
3) Visual Style:
â†’ Hero product: real photography (authentic, premium), 3D Glass version [choose one]
â†’ Cards: Apple liquid glass (85-90% transparent) with Whisper-thin borders and Subtle drop shadow for floating depth and reflecting the background color
â†’ Background stays behind cards and high blur where cards are [choose one]:
  - Ethereal: product essence, light caustics, abstract glow
  - Macro: product texture close-up, heavily blurred
  - Pattern: product repeated softly at 10-15% opacity
  - Context: relevant environment, blurred + desaturated
â†’ Add subtle motion effect
â†’ Asymmetric Bento grid, 16:9 landscape
â†’ Hero card: 28-30% | Info modules: 70-72%
4) Module Content (8 Cards):
M1 â€” Hero: Product displayed as real photo / 3D glass / stylized interpretation (choose one)in beautiful form + product name label
M2 â€” Core Benefits: 4 unique benefits + hero-color icons
M3 â€” How to Use: 4 usage methods + icons
M4 â€” Key Metrics: 5 EXACT data points
Format: [icon] [Label] [Bold Value] [Unit]
FOOD: Calories: [X] kcal/100g, Carbs: [X]g (fiber [X]g, sugar [X]g), Protein: [X]g, [Key Vitamin]: [X]mg ([X]% DV), [Key Mineral]: [X]mg ([X]% DV)
MEDICINE:Active: [name], Strength: [X] mg, Onset: [X] min, Duration: [X] hrs, Half-life: [X] hrs 
TECH:Chip: [model], Battery: [X] hrs, Weight: [X]g,[Key spec]: [value], Connectivity: [protocols]
M5 â€” Who It's For: 4 recommended groups with green checkmark icons | 3 caution groups with amber warning icons
M6 â€” Important Notes: 4 precautions + warning icons
M7 â€” Quick Reference:
â†’ FOOD: Glycemic Index + dietary tags with icons
â†’ MEDICINE: Side effects + severity with icons
â†’ TECH: Compatibility + certifications with icons
M8 â€” Did You Know: 3 facts (origin, science, global stat) + icons
Output: 1 image, 16:9 landscape, ultra-premium liquid glass infographic.
```

### No. 5: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

### No. 6: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt designed to generate an image of a vintage United States patent document from the late 1800s. #### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A vintage patent document for {argument name="invention" default="INVENTION"}, styled after late 1800s United States Patent Office filings. ### No. 8: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene
```

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 9: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured prompt for generating an ultra-realistic, high-resolution portrait of a woman with a messy bun, focusing on dramatic golden hour lighting and sharp geometric shadows. It specifies the subject's features (dirty blonde hair, blue-green eyes), clothing (oversized black hoodie, white lace bralette), pose (seated, hand touching face), and technical details (8k UHD, cinematic lighting, vertical format), aiming for an intimate and highly detailed aesthetic.

```
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "width": 2160,

  },
  "prompt_structure": {
    "subject": {
      "main_character": "beautiful young woman with shoulder-length {argument name="hair color" default="dirty blonde"} hair in a half-up half-down messy bun style",
      "facial_features": "piercing blue-green eyes full lips glowing skin with natural makeup",
      "clothing": "oversized {argument name="hoodie color" default="black"} zip-up hoodie worn off the shoulders revealing a white lace bralette or camisole underneath",
      "pose": "seated close-up portrait knees bent up one hand gently touching face near eye looking directly at camera with alluring expression"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "indoor studio setting",
      "background_elements": "plain cream or white wall with strong geometric shadow lines",
      "lighting_context": "golden hour sunset light striking the face and body creating high contrast between light and shadow"
    },
    "technical_specs": {
      "resolution": "8k uhd",
      "quality": "ultra realistic hdr",
      "lighting": "warm direct sunlight sharp shadows cinematic lighting",
      "camera_shot": "intimate portrait sharp focus on eyes highly detailed skin texture"
    }
  },
  "final_prompt_string": "Ultra realistic 8k uhd hdr portrait of a beautiful young woman with dirty blonde half-up hair and piercing blue eyes sitting against a white wall, wearing an off-shoulder black hoodie and white lace bralette, hand touching face, intense golden hour sunlight casting sharp geometric shadows across her face and the background, glowing skin texture, cinematic lighting, vertical format --ar 9:16 --stylize 750"
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt for generating a hyper-realistic, 9:16 portrait of a woman in a modern urban setting. It focuses heavily on maintaining subject consistency, realistic skin texture, specific outfit details (tied cotton shirt, tailored mini skirt), and natural daylighting for a confident, magnetic aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "aspect_ratio": "9:16",

    "hair": "long chestnut brown hair, loose with soft natural waves, slight movement from a gentle breeze",
    "face": "identical refined face with captivating eyes looking directly at camera, softly arched eyebrows, long natural lashes, refined nose, natural lips with calm confidence",
    "skin": "realistic natural skin texture with visible pores, subtle glow from daylight, no airbrush, no plastic smoothing",
    "body": "sculptural hourglass figure, defined waist, elegant hips, long toned legs with subtly sculpted calves and thighs"
  },
  "outfit": {
    "top": "light cotton shirt tied just below the bust, clean knot, relaxed fit, tasteful and effortless",
    "bottom": "high-waisted tailored mini skirt in neutral beige with structured seams",
    "footwear": "black casual ankle boots with minimalist design and matte leather finish",
    "details": "bare legs, clean feminine silhouette, premium fabric textures",
    "accessories": {
      "jewelry": "small gold hoops and a delicate bracelet",
      "bag": "optional small crossbody leather bag in neutral tone"
    }
  },
  "pose": "front-facing stance with one boot placed against a wall at hip height, leg elegantly bent, hips subtly angled, shoulders relaxed, torso upright, direct confident gaze into camera",
  "setting": {
    "location": "sunlit urban street with textured stone wall",
    "environment": "clean architectural lines, light-colored pavement, soft shadows from nearby buildings, minimal traffic",
    "background": "softly blurred city details with greenery hints and bright sky"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "radiant natural daylight",
    "sources": [
      "soft direct sunlight illuminating face and legs",
      "gentle fill light bouncing from light walls",
      "subtle rim light outlining hair and silhouette"
    ],
    "effect": "bright but balanced exposure, natural highlights, gentle shadows defining curves without harsh contrast"
  },
  "camera": {
    "style": "high-end fashion lifestyle photography",
    "perspective": "straight-on eye-level framing with slight upward tilt to elongate legs",
    "focus": "sharp focus on subject with smooth background falloff",
    "depth_of_field": "moderate, cinematic separation"
  },
  "style": {
    "aesthetic": "modern urban chic",
    "mood": "confident, luminous, magnetic, effortless",
    "realism": "hyper-realistic and tactile",
    "avoid": [
      "plastic skin",
      "studio flash look",
```

### No. 34: Infographic / Edu Visual - Hyper-realistic Indonesian Food Infographic Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured JSON prompt for generating a hyper-realistic food infographic image of an Indonesian dish, featuring levitating ingredients (meat, tofu, herbs) above a bowl, emphasizing cinematic studio lighting and editorial layout.

```
{

      "cuisine": "Indonesian",

        "Fresh herbs",

        "Lime",
        "Garlic",
        "Fried shallots"
      ]
    },

      "layout": "Clean vertical composition",
      "arrangement": "Realistic gravity-defying/floating elements",
      "background": "Rustic wooden surface",
      "visual_hierarchy": "Bowl anchored at bottom, ingredients rising vertically"
    },
    "graphic_design_elements": {
      "labels": "Clear Indonesian text",
      "lines": "Thin white pointing lines",
      "style": "Editorial infographic layout, professional food magazine style"
    },
    "lighting_and_mood": {
      "lighting": "Cinematic studio lighting",
      "color_palette": "Warm tones",
      "effects": "Dramatic steam, motion-frozen ingredients"
    },
    "technical_specs": {
      "camera_settings": "Shallow depth of field, sharp focus, DSLR look",
      "details": "Ultra-detailed textures",
```

### No. 37: Infographic / Edu Visual - Infographic prompt for 'Monday to Sunday' infinite loop manga

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to create a comical, anime-style infographic showing the infinite loop of a week, from the despair of Monday to the brief joy of the weekend, using a 7-segment circular pizza-cut layout while strictly maintaining character consistency from a reference image.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Character Reference Specification]
Must use the character from the reference image.
Must depict the same person in all panels.
Facial features, hairstyle, eye shape, and atmosphere must be perfectly consistent.
Changing the person, face, or hairstyle is prohibited.
Clothing may change for each day of the week, but the character itself must be the same.
Even if deformed, the character must be instantly recognizable as the person in the reference image.

[Overall Concept]
An anime illustration representing one week from Monday to Sunday,
in a perfectly circular shape.

[Composition/Layout]
ãƒ»The entire circle must be divided into exactly 7 pizza-cut segments.
ãƒ»6 or 12 divisions are prohibited.
ãƒ»Exactly 7 equal sectors.
ãƒ»Infographic-style layout.
ãƒ»All 7 panels must connect naturally.

[Order of Days (Strictly Enforced - Clockwise)]
MONDAY â†’ TUESDAY â†’ WEDNESDAY â†’ THURSDAY â†’ FRIDAY â†’ SATURDAY â†’ SUNDAY â†’ returns to MONDAY

[Circulation Expression]
ãƒ»Place a thick circular arrow on the outer circumference of the circle.
ãƒ»Clockwise direction.
ãƒ»Emphasize that the week repeats infinitely.

[Character Design]
ãƒ»Comical anime character with strong deformation.
ãƒ»Chibi-style body shape.
ãƒ»Large head and small body.
ãƒ»Short limbs.
ãƒ»Expressions are extreme and gag-oriented.
ãƒ»Cute and exaggerated reactions.

[Text Rules]
ãƒ»Only English day names are placed in each panel:
"MONDAY", "TUESDAY", "WEDNESDAY", "THURSDAY",
"FRIDAY", "SATURDAY", "SUNDAY".
ãƒ»No dialogue, speech bubbles, or Japanese text whatsoever.
ãƒ»Day names must be bold, easy to read, and without distortion.
ãƒ»Placed along the shape of each panel.

[Depiction of Each Day]

MONDAY:
Deformed office worker (OL) in a suit.
Messy hair, dead eyes.
Holding two large coffees.

TUESDAY:
Working silently on a computer.
Surrounded by a mountain of documents taller than herself.

WEDNESDAY:
Working late overtime.
Dark office, night view outside the window.
Slumped posture, utterly exhausted.

THURSDAY:
Comical expression of the soul leaving the mouth.
A transparent, cute soul floats up from the body.
Depicting extreme fatigue as a gag.

FRIDAY:
High-tension expression.
Taking off her jacket,
Holding a large beer mug overflowing with foam.
Festive atmosphere.

SATURDAY:
Out happily with friends in casual clothes.
Energetic pose, jumping.
Bright and lively atmosphere.

SUNDAY:
Lying down on the bed as if collapsing.
The word "MONDAY" is visible on the smartphone screen.
Exaggerated despair.

[Art Style/Quality]
ãƒ»Comical anime style with strong deformation.
ãƒ»Thick line art.
ãƒ»Simple shading.
ãƒ»Bright and pop color scheme.
ãƒ»Expressions are very easy to understand.
ãƒ»High-quality illustration.

[Negative Prompts]
ãƒ»Realistic style, photorealistic expression.
ãƒ»Changes in character's face or hairstyle.
ãƒ»Composition other than 7 divisions.
ãƒ»Disruption of the day order.
ãƒ»Japanese day names.
ãƒ»Dialogue, speech bubbles.
ãƒ»Distortion or collapse of text.
ãƒ»Square panel division.
```

### No. 42: Infographic / Edu Visual - Helical Tower Sculpture Prompt for Visualizing Historical Evolution

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-level prompt designed to visualize the historical progression of a topic (like literature or computing) as a massive, helical tower sculpture in a dark museum setting. It requires deconstructing the topic into four vertical eras, specifying architectural details for each level, and including 1:50 scale figures actively working on the technology of their time, resulting in a detailed 3D museum installation art piece.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Do this for literature: <instruction>
 
Input A is a Topic with a clear historical progression (e.g., {argument name="topic" default="Literature"}, Medicine, Flight, Computing).
Deconstruct the history into   4 Vertical Eras  :
     Level 1 (The Foundation - Bottom):  The Ancient Origin.
         (e.g., Literature -> Stone Tablets & Scrolls. Flight -> Da Vinci Wings & Kites). 
     Level 2 (The Tradition - Lower Mid):  The Medieval/Renaissance Era.
         (e.g., Literature -> Scriptorium & Monks. Flight -> Hot Air Balloons). 
     Level 3 (The Revolution - Upper Mid):  The Industrial Age.
         (e.g., Literature -> Printing Press & Newspapers. Flight -> Propeller Planes). 
     Level 4 (The Horizon - Top):  The Digital/Future Age.
         (e.g., Literature -> Holographic Data & VR. Flight -> Spacecraft & Ion Thrusters). 

  2.  Container (The Rotunda):  
Goal: "Museum Installation" 3D Art.
     The Object:  A massive, freestanding   Helical Tower Sculpture   standing in a dark museum hall.
     The Base:  A circular Bronze Plinth with a gold plaque reading: "THE EVOLUTION OF [{argument name="topic" default="INPUT A"}]".

  3. The Structure (The Spiral):  
     The Spine:  A central mechanical or architectural pillar supports the structure.
     The Ramp:  A continuous, wide   Spiral Ramp   winds upwards around the central pillar (like the Tower of Babel or DNA).
     The Vignettes:  Along the ramp at each level, detailed   Architectural Dioramas   are built:
         Bottom:  Stone arches, caves, or temples.
         Middle:  Timber frames, brick factories, or iron trusses.
         Top:  Floating glass platforms, laser grids, or cloud computing nodes.

  4. The Narrative Scale (The Population):  
     Scale:  1:50 Scale Figures.
     Action:  At every level, figures are actively "working" on the technology of their time (e.g., Scribes writing, Mechanics wrenching, Cyborgs interfacing).
```

```
      ],
      "weather": "overcast"

    },
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

```
        "purpose": "STYLE_COMPOSITION_COLORGRADE_ANCHOR",
        "strict_lock": true,
        "preserve_vibe": true,
        "preserve_palette": true,
        "preserve_lighting": true
      },

        "strict_lock": true,

        "no_identity_blending": true,
        "no_age_shift": true,
        "preserve_skin_texture": true
      },
      "reference_face_male": {
        "source": "UPLOAD_REFERENCE_FACE_MALE (OPTIONAL)",
        "purpose": "FACE_IDENTITY_LOCK",
        "strict_lock": true,
        "face_similarity_priority": "MAX",
        "identity_lock_strength": 0.995,
        "no_identity_blending": true,
        "no_age_shift": true,
        "preserve_skin_texture": true
      }
    },
    "output": {
      "format": "single_image_collage",
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution": "high",
      "no_text": true,
      "no_logos": true,
      "no_ui": true,
      "no_watermark": true,

          "panel_3_topdown_centerline_lie",
          "panel_4_pov_racket_foreground"
        ],
        "panel_separators": "thin clean borders, no captions"
      }
    },
    "global_style": {
      "aesthetic": "romantic sporty editorial, cinematic lifestyle",
      "time_of_day": "golden hour / late afternoon",
      "color_grade": "warm filmic tones, soft contrast, natural skin",
      "photorealism": "maximum",
      "skin_texture": "natural, no beauty filter",
      "wardrobe": {
        "female": "white tennis skirt + white fitted top, white socks and sneakers",
        "male": "white polo shirt + beige shorts, white sneakers",
        "notes": "clean, minimal, sporty-chic"
      },
      "props": {
        "tennis_rackets": "classic wooden/neutral tone rackets",
        "tennis_balls": "a few scattered near net/center court"
      }
    },
    "scene": {
      "location": "outdoor tennis court with net and chain-link fence",
      "background": "trees and park elements softly out of focus, warm sunlight",
      "environment": {
        "court_color": "muted blue/green hard court",
        "mood": "soft, romantic, playful"
      }
    },
    "panels": {
```

```
      "no_face_warp":true,
      "no_warped_limbs":true

      "no_modern_objects":true,
      "no_text":true,
      "no_logos":true
    },

      "jewelry_hair_nails":{
        "female":{
          "hair":"partially covered or tightly pinned back, loose strands blowing in the wind",
          "nails":"short, natural, clean, no polish",
          "jewelry":"minimal or none, period-appropriate only"
        },
        "male":{
          "jewelry":"none"
        }
      },

      "camera":"85mm cinematic portrait lens, close-medium framing, faces and hands in sharp focus while storm softens the background",

      "lighting":"overcast storm light with soft directional highlights on faces, subtle contrast, no harsh shadows",

      "color_palette":"cool storm blues and grays contrasted with warm natural skin tones",
```

```
â€œIn this day and age, interspecies marriage is common! Differences in lifespan or species don't matter when it comes to love!â€

The man looks serious, sensing something. Positioned on the left side of the screen.

Elf
â€œHmph, look at this, and tell me if you can still say the same?â€

Human Man

Panel 4

Elf Woman
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical prompt for generating an extreme close-up macro product image of pharmaceutical capsules and a single oval softgel suspended in midair. #### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
IMAGE: Frame & Composition: The camera presents an extreme close-up macro composition with a straight-on, perpendicular viewing angle to the subject plane; the frame is tightly cropped on multiple capsules and a single oval softgel suspended in midair, with no visible container or support; objects are distributed diagonally across the frame, creating a loose radial balance around the central softgel, which occupies the visual and spatial center; several capsules are partially cropped by the frame edges, reinforcing a floating, weightless arrangement; depth cues suggest all elements are within a narrow spatial range, with slight size variation indicating minimal distance differences from the lens. Lighting & Atmosphere: A controlled studio key light originates from the lower left, producing strong specular highlights along the curved surfaces of the transparent capsules and a concentrated luminous hotspot within the amber softgel; shadow transitions are smooth and soft, indicating a diffused light source with moderate directional bias; reflections are crisp but not harsh, suggesting polished surfaces without environmental haze; the background remains evenly lit with no visible bloom, fog, or particulate atmosphere. Subject Geometry & Materiality: The primary subject is an elongated, oval softgel oriented horizontally with a slight upward tilt on its right edge; its gelatin shell is transparent amber with a smooth, high-gloss surface and a visible internal meniscus line; surrounding it are cylindrical two-piece capsules oriented at varied angles, each composed of semi-transparent shells filled with fine granular powder; the powder exhibits uneven density, settling toward the lower halves of the capsules, creating subtle tonal gradients; shell seams are visible as fine circumferential lines; surface reflections reveal smooth plastic-like material with micro-scratches and minute dust inclusions visible under macro magnification. Environmental Layering: The foreground and midground are occupied entirely by the capsules and softgel, all rendered in sharp focus with minimal depth separation; no object fully occludes another, though overlaps occur at shallow angles; the background is a uniform gradient field transitioning from {argument name="background color top" default="deep blue"} at the top to a {argument name="background color bottom" default="lighter blue-gray"} toward the bottom, completely out of focus and free of discernible texture or structure; there are no environmental props or surfaces present. Technical Artifacts & Color: The color palette is limited and controlled, dominated by warm amber and beige tones of the capsules contrasted against a cool blue gradient background; saturation is moderate, with the softgel exhibiting the highest chroma; image grain is minimal and fine, consistent with a high-resolution studio capture; no chromatic aberration, motion blur, or compositing edges are visible; highlights are clean with smooth roll-of
```

### No. 94: E-commerce Main Image - High-End Concept Art Magazine Editorial Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt template for generating a high-end, glossy editorial photograph of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized by a brand. It specifies ultra-premium materials, cinematic studio lighting (Phase One camera, 100mm macro lens), and a strict layout for text and logo placement, designed to visualize concept magazine ideas.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[BRAND NAME]: 
A high-end, glossy concept art magazine editorial photograph of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by the brand.

**1. The Concept & Object (AI Invention):**
Based on the design philosophy, heritage, and material vocabulary of the specified brand, the AI must invent a novel utility product (NOT standard clothing, shoes, or bags). Examples could be home goods, tech accessories, tools, or sporting equipment, reinterpretated through the brand's lens. The object should feel sculptural yet functional.

**2. Materials & Details (Hyper-Premium):**
The object is constructed from ultra-premium, highly tactile materials characteristic of the brand (e.g., patinated exotic leathers, brushed aerospace-grade titanium, sculpted matte ceramics, molded carbon fiber, or technical high-fashion textiles). Every detail is hyper-realistic: visible stitching, microscopic material grain, precision engravings, and complex texture contrasts.

**3. Photography & Lighting (Cinematic Studio):**
Shot on a medium format Phase One camera with a 100mm macro lens. Extremely shallow depth of field, with sharp focus on the hero details of the object and a creamy, smooth bokeh background. The lighting is sophisticated studio softbox lighting: gentle, enveloping fill light with precise rim lighting to accentuate contours and material textures.

**4. Environment:**
A seamless, impeccably clean studio cyclorama background in a pure, ultra-light pastel tone (e.g., desaturated mint, pale blush, or off-white), free of shadows.

**5. Layout & UI Elements (Strict Placement):**
- **Bottom Right Corner:** A small, understated, monochrome gray logo of the {argument name="brand name" default="BRAND NAME"}.
```

### No. 106: Game Asset - Chibi Character Operating a Cyber Window Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate an anime-style chibi girl operating a semi-transparent window in cyberspace. The prompt includes specific details about the character's expression, hair, AR glasses, outfit, pose, surrounding objects, background, and art style, including text overlays.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
## Overall Concept
concept: "A cute, smiling chibi character girl engrossed in operating a semi-transparent window (display) floating in cyberspace"

## Details of the Main Character
subject:
  type: "Chibi character in anime style"
  reference: "Character design should be based on the character design reference sheet attached in the image"
  expression: "A beaming smile with sparkling eyes, full of discovery and joy"
  hair:
    details: "Part of the hair faintly glows like data particles"
  wearables:
    - item: "AR Glasses"
      type: "Frameless visor style"
      material: "Highly transparent, semi-transparent material with a crystal-like texture"
      details: "The rim of the glasses glows with a thin neon blue line, projecting information into her field of view"
  outfit:
    style: "Geometric patterns resembling electronic circuits are printed in cyan on the inside of the cuffs"
  direction: "Facing the left side of the image"

## Character Action and Pose
action:
  verb: "Operating the window (display)"
  pose: "Floating gently in cyberspace, leaning slightly forward, operating the semi-transparent window (display) floating in the air"
  hands: "Lightly moving fingertips, operating the semi-transparent window (display) floating in the air"

## Surrounding Objects
objects:
  - item: "Multiple semi-transparent windows floating in the air"
    type: "Semi-transparent interface"
    shape: "Wide screen with gentle curves"
    content: "A colorful list is visible, transparently, within the window."
    details: "Since the window (display) is semi-transparent, the character and background behind it are visible through it"

## Background and Environment
environment:
  setting: "Abstract and minimal cyberspace"
  background:
    color: "Black"
    details:
      - "A white starburst (with very thin, sharp spikes) is drawn behind the character, centered on the character."
      - "Small particles of data light and semi-transparent cubes are slowly drifting around her"
    text:
      - "Upper right of the screen: Large vertical text: 'After all, Sticky ToC....' (The text 'Sticky ToC' should be displayed horizontally.)"
      - "Upper left of the screen: Large vertical text: 'Sticky ToC \n solves everything....!!' (The text 'Sticky ToC' should be displayed horizontally.)"

## Art Style and Quality
style:
  art_style: "High-quality anime illustration, smooth line art and vibrant colors"
  lighting: "The character herself and the window (display) she is operating are the main light sources. Soft reflected light from the display hits her face and body. Overall bright and clean impression."
  color_palette: "White base, with pastel pink, emerald green, cyber blue, and cyan as accent colors"
  effects: "Moderate use of glow and bloom effects"
  quality: "Highest quality, masterpiece, ultra-high resolution, detailed"
```

```
0â€“4 seconds:
Slow, dramatic buildup. The hamster struggles to initiate the lift â€” muscles tense, fur slightly trembling, paws tightening on the bar. Subtle body shake, controlled strain, deep focus. No camera shake. No text. No flashy effects.
4â€“8 seconds:
The hamster successfully deadlifts the barbell in one smooth, powerful motion, lifting it from the floor to full standing lockout. Chest up, shoulders back, bar held firmly at hip level. The effort turns into quiet triumph.
Cinematic low front angle throughout to exaggerate scale and power.
Shallow depth of field with a modern gym environment softly blurred in the background.
Cool neutral gym lighting with realistic reflections on metal plates and soft shadows on the floor.
Style:
Hyper-realistic, premium movie realism, high contrast, clean motion, no distortion, no surreal physics, no bar intersecting the body, no camera jumps, no visual noise.
```

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
